Distinctive two-handled pewter Chimes Mugs near the fireplace are used for Chimes Nights.     Pivoting to Management Consulting

    Hi Terina, I hope you're staying well and safe during these covid-times. I thoroughly enjoyed reading your Feb 26th article in Forbes Careers (https://www.forbes.com/sites/terinaallen/2020/02/26/this-is-what-it-takes-to-become-a-successful-management-consultant/#2c2ebb6a4ce1). It was organized, succinct, and tangible.  My question for you is specifically regarding the section discussing the 4 levels of education and experience in management consulting - are there alternative ways to pivot into the industry besides the normal campus recruiting tracks (i.e., step 1)? For a personal example: I, along with what I presume to be millions of others, am seeking to pivot out of my current position in the hospitality industry by upskilling in project management and data analysis, and leveraging the skills I've gained in training and hospitality management. Are there resources you could recommend that might provide guidance toward "breaking into" the management consulting industry, given my several years' experiences in a different one? Thank you for your time! :-) Alex Newton
